itemprop="image" height="1599" width="2400" title="Students 2" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h2> Standardized Features for Easy and Accessible 3D Printing </h2> <img src="https://www.makerbot.com/wp-content/plugins/bb-plugin/img/pixel.png" alt="" itemprop="image" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <p>To ensure easy, accessible 3D printing, the MakerBot Replicator+ comes with the Smart Extruder+ and all the standard features of its predecessor. A few of those features include an LCD display, an on-board camera, as well as USB, Ethernet, and Wi-Fi connection.</p>   <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/reliability_module_4.jpg" alt="MakerBot Replicator+ Gantry" itemprop="image" height="500" width="520" title="MakerBot Replicator+ Gantry" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h2> Engineered and Tested for Greater Reliability </h2> <p>The MakerBot Replicator+ prints 30% faster than its predecessor and offers a 25% larger build volume. For greater reliability and precision, it features improved hardware, like a redesigned gantry and z-stage.</p> <p>To ensure consistent performance, our new 3D printers and their subsystems were re-engineered and rigorously tested for 380,000+ hours across multiple facilities.</p> <h2> Combines With Powerful Workflow Tools to Streamline the 3D Printing Process </h2> <p>Save time and accelerate iteration by pairing the Replicator+ with MakerBot Print software and MakerBot Mobile. The Replicator+ is Cloud-enabled so you can control it remotely with MakerBot Print or the MakerBot Mobile app. With MakerBot Print, you can import Native CAD parts and assemblies, auto-arrange them during print preparation, and then print them on one or more printers. To get started printing quickly and easily, MakerBot Mobile offers an all-new guided wireless setup.</p> <p> </p> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/powerful_tools_module_5.jpg" alt="powerful_tools_module_5" itemprop="image" height="495" width="880" title="powerful_tools_module_5" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h2> Flex Build Plate with Grip Build Surface </h2> <p>With the new Grip Surface, prints adhere better, resulting in reduced warping and curling. Prints are also easier to remove with the new bendable Flex Build Plate. The large build plate is also factory-leveled so your Replicator+ is ready to produce right out of the box.</p> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/BUILD-PLATE-REPLICATOR-Flexible-Giza.png" alt="BUILD-PLATE-REPLICATOR-Flexible-Giza" itemprop="image" title="BUILD-PLATE-REPLICATOR-Flexible-Giza" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/smart_extruder_module_7.jpg" alt="MakerBot Smart Extruder+" itemprop="image" height="602" width="580" title="MakerBot Smart Extruder+" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h2> Includes the MakerBot Smart Extruder+ </h2> <p>Double the warranty of its predecessor, the Smart Extruder+ is a culmination of product design, technology and 160,000+ hours of rigorous testing that delivers dependable, consistent performance with superior results using MakerBot PLA (polylactic acid) Material.</p> <a href="https://store.makerbot.com/3d-printers/extruders/smart-extruder-for-makerbot-replicator-replicator-mini/" target="_self" role="button" rel="noopener noreferrer"> SHOP NOW </a> <h2> On-Board Camera </h2> <p>Remotely monitor your print progress from <a href="https://www.makerbot.com/print">MakerBot Print</a> and MakerBot Mobile. Our platform allows you to view the entire process, resulting in unparalleled print quality.</p> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/camera_module_8.jpg" alt="MakerBot Replicator+ On-Board Camera" itemprop="image" height="608" width="1080" title="MakerBot Replicator+ On-Board Camera" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/lcd_module_9.jpg" alt="MakerBot Replicator+ LCD Display" itemprop="image" height="512" width="1080" title="MakerBot Replicator+ LCD Display" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h2> Ease of Use via the LCD Display and Dial </h2> <p>Along with an intuitive dial, the LCD display allows you to set up and maintain your 3D printer, preview print files, and easily access your object library.</p> <h2> More Features </h2> <p><img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/icon-flexibile-connectivity.png" alt="" width="72" height="72" /></p> <h3>Flexible Connectivity</h3> <p>Send print files to your 3D printer via Wi-Fi, USB, Ethernet, or with a USB drive. Control your printer settings via MakerBot Print or remotely with MakerBot Mobile.</p> <p><img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/software_module_9.svg" alt="" /></p> <h3>Advanced Software</h3> <p>Control multiple printers from MakerBot Print so you can print on multiple build plates sequentially or simultaneously. Store, organize, and access a wide range of 3D design files in your personal Cloud-enabled library. MakerBot Print is free downloadable software that’s compatible with Mac, and Windows computers.</p> <p><img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/support_module_9.svg" alt="" /></p> <h3>MakerBot Support</h3> <p>MakerBot Support offers comprehensive <a href="https://www.makerbot.com/makercare/">MakerCare</a> coverage plans and responsive expertise from those who know high quality MakerBot products best.       • TOUGH<!-- wp:fl-builder/layout --> <img src="https://3qcbdntxdyb43ubh6h0b0qgz-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/tough-grey-front.jpg" alt="tough grey front" itemprop="image" height="3002" width="3459" title="tough grey front" onerror="this.style.display='none'" /> <h3> MakerBot TOUGH </h3> <h5> Durable, tough parts, office-friendly printing </h5> <p>Tough is a material that is great for mid-stage prototypes because of its ease of use and office-friendliness.
